 Book: Wake up! Wake up Go ahead Author: Sandeepkumar Salunkheprakash: Prabhat Publication Price: Rs 125 (paperback) Every person in the world desires to succeed in their respective fields, but not everyone is successful
 safalataa ke maarg main jo sabase badi baadha aati he, vah 'baahar' nahin, balki 'bheetar' hi sthit hoti he
 In this story, a lively and true story of achieving success by recovering from every moment of duality in the mind is presented in an interesting way
 pustak main prerak prasangon or sukhtiyon kaa behatar istemaal kiya gaya he
 How an ordinary teenager dreams of becoming a big officer, what obstacles come in the way and how he can overcome these obstacles and achieve his destination, that is at the center of the book
 lekhak swami vivekanand kii jeevani se kaaphi prerit hai
 He has mentioned it in clear words
 vichaar hi hamen mahaan banaate hanyah ek swayansiddh tathy he ki hamaare vichaar hi hamen mahaan banaate hai
 Good results of good thoughts, bad results of bad thoughts
 hamaara bhavishya inhen vichaaron kii buniyaad par tikaa hota he
 But an ordinary human being cannot distinguish good and bad at many points of life
 yaa sabakuch jaanate-samajhate hue bhi nindaneey kaamon se khud ko alag nahin kar paata
 In this book, the author has opened the pages of his life in front of everyone and tries to explain that if we overcome our dilemma at the right time, then it becomes very easy to reach the destination
 sabase bada aparaadh he 'pragyaparaadh'agar koi bhul anjaane main ho jaati he, to vyakti khud ko maaf karne main der nahin lagaataa
 But the burden of mistake or mistake that is done on purpose is the most difficult job in the world
 soi hui aatma tab bhi sabakuch maun hokar nihaar rahi hoti he
 In scriptures, it is called 'pragyapradha'
 lekhak ne apane jivan ke kuch vaise prasangon ko zikr karke kitaab kii ahmiyat or badha di he
 See these lines: 'now i started going to the cinema every day
 badi chuttee ke baad saare period se main nadaarad rahata
 i would not feel sad that my studies were sinking
 
 
 main pehle kaa ‘sandip’ na rahaa tha
 a powerful current was taking me away at full speed
 ’khaas baat yah he ki lekhak ne duvidhaon ke janjaal se nikalakar sankalp lene kaa behtareen udhaaharan saamne rakhaa he
 Why read this book 
 
 sawaal uthta he ki jab prerak vyaktitv or prerana dene vaali duusari kitaaben pehle se hi maujuud hai, to is kitaab ko kyon padhaa jaae
 Actually, the nature of our mind is such that it does not associate itself with the success of the great people of the world as a great divine miracle or destiny
 khud mahaan banane kii uski aakanksha janm to leti he, par phalne-phoolne kii bajaae dam tod detii he
 But when he sees someone becoming extraordinary from ordinary in his own time, he is more motivated
 aisi sthiti main vah us vyaktitv se khud ko zyada acchhee tarah jod paata he
 Then nothing seems impossible, every work seems possible
 yahi is kitaab kii sabase badi upyogita he
 Why not read this book 
 
 agar jivan main or koi kamyaabi hasil karne kii aakanksha na bachi ho, aapane thaan liya he ki jo he, thik he, to yah kitaab shaayad kii aapaki koi madad kar paae

 devuthni ekadshi ko devuthan ekadshi (devuthan Ekadashi), hariprabodhini ekadshi (hariprabodhini Ekadashi) yaa prabodhini ekadshi (prabodhini Ekadashi) ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he
 According to the Hindu beliefs, on this Ekadashi (ekadashi), Sri Hari Vishnu, the practitioner of creation, wakes up after four months of yoga sleep
 manyata he ki is din tulsi vivaah ke madhyam se unka ahvaahan kar unhen jagaaya jaataa he
 On the day of Devuthani Ekadashi, the marriage of Lord Shaligram and Tulsi saplings is done by Hindu customs
 tulsi vivaah (tulsi Vivah) kaa aayojan karnaa atyant mangalakaari or shubh mana jaataa he
 It is said that on the day of Devuthani Ekadashi, offering Tulsi Dal to Lord Vishnu and marrying Tulsi with Shaligram eliminates all the pain and the devotee receives the special grace of Shri Hari
 unki prarthana sunakar bhagwaan vishnu ne vrinda kaa pativrata dharm bhang karne kaa nishchay kiya
 He took the form of Jalandhar and touched Vrinda with deceit
 vrinda kaa pati jalandhar, devataaon se parakram se yuddh kar rahaa tha, lekin vrinda kaa satitv nasht hote hi maaraa gaya
 As soon as Vrinda's saintliness dissolved, Jalandhar's head fell into her courtyard
 jab vrinda ne yah dekha to krodhit hokar jaananaa chaha ki phir jise usne sparsh kiya vah koun he
 Visnu was standing in front of him
 usne bhagwaan vishnu ko shaap de diya, ''jis prakaar tumne chal se mujhe pati viyog diya he, usee prakaar tumhaari patni kaa bhi chhalpurvak haran hoga or stri viyog sahane ke liye tum bhi mrityu lok main janm loge
